# ios-audio-gatekeeping-study

We start with a listing of AUv3 AudioUnit apps.

### Background: A problem arises when an increasing number of mechanisms disrupt the free market for niche products (in this case, the iOS audio market) in a variety of ways. This ranges from (more or less) incomplete listings to active market manipulation by self-proclaimed experts and questionable, interest-driven communities.

Furthermore, we will reveal through studies which mechanisms have developed in this niche market and how they manipulate the market.

## An Initial Search for ‚AUv3’

This extract was created with AudioApp Researcher Pro - 2026-07-11 06:16:03 +0000.

(Note: The list is sorted by the date of the last update or release. Please be aware that due to Apple's inadequate search API, it is not easy or even safe to compile a complete list of available AudioUnits. This is part of the issue encountered. We are therefore striving to develop a method for listing these niche apps as completely and independently as possible. )
